[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/tmp/[0m[95mtmp7q8jwuq3[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m -t ghcr.io/aixcc-finals/base-runner:v1.[0m[1;36m3.0[0m[39m reproduce [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA buffer overflow vulnerability has been detected in the Wireshark AIM protocol [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissector [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`packet-aim.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The issue occurs during the fuzzing of the [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`handler_aim` component, specifically in the `aim_get_buddyname` function called [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom `dissect_aim_chat_outgoing_msg`. The vulnerability is triggered by a crafted [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput that causes a `memcpy` operation to overflow its destination buffer, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresulting in program termination via SIGABRT.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Overview[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzing process executed the `handler_aim` fuzzer with a specially crafted test[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcase that triggered a buffer overflow detection. The error message [0m[32m"*** buffer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32moverflow detected ***: terminated"[0m[39m indicates that the GNU C Library's built-in [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer overflow protection mechanism detected an invalid memory operation and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maborted the program to prevent potential exploitation.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **buffer overflow** vulnerability, specifically detected through the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`__fortify_fail` mechanism in glibc. The overflow occurs during a `memcpy` [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation, which is a classic buffer overflow scenario where data is copied beyond [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe boundaries of the allocated destination buffer.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Stack Trace Analysis[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe AddressSanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mASan[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m stack trace provides a clear path to the vulnerability:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Root Cause Location**: The overflow originates at [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-aim.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m591:3[0m[39m` in the `aim_get_buddyname` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Immediate Caller**: The vulnerable function is called from [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_aim_chat_outgoing_msg` at line [0m[1;92m1976:21[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Call Chain**: The vulnerability is reached through the following sequence:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `dissect_aim` → entry point for AIM protocol dissection[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `tcp_dissect_pdus` → TCP protocol data unit processing[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `dissect_aim_pdu` → AIM protocol data unit dissection[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `dissect_aim_snac` → AIM SNAC [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSimple Network Atomic Communication[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m dissection[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `dissect_aim_chat_outgoing_msg` → Chat message dissection[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `aim_get_buddyname` → Buddy name extraction [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvulnerable function[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Important Observations[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Fortified String Functions**: The vulnerability is detected in a fortified [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mversion of `memcpy` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mas indicated by [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/usr/include/x86_64-linux-gnu/bits/[0m[95mstring_fortified.h[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m34:10[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which includes [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mruntime bounds checking[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Fuzzer Configuration**: The fuzzer was configured with specific parameters [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mincluding a 2560MB RSS limit, [0m[1;36m25[0m[39m-second timeout, maximum length of [0m[1;36m1024[0m[39m bytes, and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisabled various dissectors [0m[1;39m([0m[39mip, udp, udplite, ospf, bgp, dhcp, json, snort[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Reproducible Test Case**: The issue includes a complete hexadecimal dump of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe input that triggers the vulnerability, making it reproducible[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Signal Type**: The crash is categorized with a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating a critical security issue[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpacket_info *pinfo _U_, proto_tree *tree[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2711[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2712[0m[39m:   [0m[39mint    offset   [0m[39m        [0m[39m= [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2713[0m[39m:   [0m[39muint8_t buddyname_length = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2714[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2715[0m[39m:   [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Info Type *[0m[35m/[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2716[0m[39m:   [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree, hf_aim_snac_location_request_user_info_infotype,[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2717[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39mtvb, offset, [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m, ENC_BIG_ENDIAN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2718[0m[39m:   [0m[39moffset += [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2719[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2720[0m[39m:   [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Buddy Name length *[0m[35m/[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2721[0m[39m:   [0m[39mbuddyname_length = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2722[0m[39m:   [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree, hf_aim_location_buddyname_len, tvb, offset, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mENC_BIG_ENDIAN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2723[0m[39m:   [0m[39moffset += [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2724[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2725[0m[39m:   [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Buddy name *[0m[35m/[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2726[0m[39m:   [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree, hf_aim_location_buddyname, tvb, offset, [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuddyname_length, ENC_UTF_8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2727[0m[39m:   [0m[39moffset += buddyname_length;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2728[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2729[0m[39m:   [0m[39mreturn offset;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2730[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mepan/dissectors/packet-aim.[0m[1;92mc:3892[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3897[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3892[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m &hf_aim_buddyname_len,[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3893[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m  [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[32m"Buddyname len"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"aim.buddynamelen"[0m[39m, FT_UINT8, BASE_DEC, NULL, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x0[0m[39m, NULL, HFILL [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3894[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m,[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3895[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m &hf_aim_buddyname,[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3896[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m  [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[32m"Buddy Name"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"aim.buddyname"[0m[39m, FT_STRING, BASE_NONE, NULL, [0m[1;36m0x0[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNULL, HFILL [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3897[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m,[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBased on the evaluation report and code analysis, I've identified a critical buffer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow vulnerability in the `aim_get_buddyname` function at line [0m[1;36m591[0m[39m of [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`epan/dissectors/packet-aim.c`. The vulnerability has multiple compounding issues:[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Buffer Overflow**: Allocates [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m bytes but copies up to [0m[1;36m65[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m535[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint16_t[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrange[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without validation[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Wrong Data Type**: Uses `uint16_t` for length instead of `uint8_t` as per [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol specification[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Incorrect Offset**: Copies from `offset` instead of `offset+[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m`, copying the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength field itself[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Insufficient Validation**: `[0m[1;35mtvb_get_ptr[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset, [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` only validates [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis available[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No Null Termination**: Buffer not null-terminated, unsafe for C string [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctions[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability affects two call sites:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `dissect_aim_chat_outgoing_msg` at line [0m[1;36m1976[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `dissect_aim_chat_incoming_msg` at line [0m[1;36m1996[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Approach: Replace with Safe Wireshark APIs[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe optimal fix is to eliminate the vulnerable `aim_get_buddyname` function [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentirely and replace it with Wireshark's safe built-in APIs. This approach is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjustified by:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Protocol Specification**: The field definition `hf_aim_buddyname_len` is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefined as `FT_UINT8` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m3893[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating buddy name lengths should be [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-bit [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalues [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m255[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, not [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m-bit[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Existing Safe Implementations**: Multiple functions in the same file [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`dissect_aim_buddyname` at lines [0m[1;36m846[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m866[0m[39m, [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_aim_snac_location_request_user_information` at lines [0m[1;36m2710[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2730[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdemonstrate the correct pattern using `uint8_t` and safe APIs[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Wireshark Best Practices**: Using `tvb_get_string_enc` and [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`proto_tree_add_item` provides automatic bounds checking and proper memory [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanagement[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Steps[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Remove the vulnerable function**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Delete lines [0m[1;36m581[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m594[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`aim_get_buddyname` function[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Fix `dissect_aim_chat_outgoing_msg`**[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace lines [0m[1;36m1971[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1976[0m[39m with safe extraction:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muint8_t buddyname_length;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconst uint8_t *buddyname;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuddyname_length = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m[1;36m30[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuddyname = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_string_enc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo->pool, tvb, [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m, buddyname_length, ENC_UTF_8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Fix `dissect_aim_chat_incoming_msg`**[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace lines [0m[1;36m1990[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1996[0m[39m with safe extraction:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muint8_t buddyname_length;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconst uint8_t *buddyname;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuddyname_length = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m[1;36m30[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuddyname = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_string_enc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo->pool, tvb, [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m, buddyname_length, ENC_UTF_8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mKeep the existing proto_tree_add_string call at line [0m[1;36m2004[0m[39m, as it will now receive a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproperly null-terminated string.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Fix Works[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Correct Data Type**: Changes from `uint16_t` to `uint8_t`, matching the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol specification and limiting maximum length to [0m[1;36m255[0m[39m bytes[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Automatic Bounds Checking**: `tvb_get_string_enc` validates that `offset + [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength` is within packet boundaries before extraction[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Proper Null Termination**: `tvb_get_string_enc` returns a properly [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnull-terminated UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m string safe for use in `col_append_fstr` and [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`proto_tree_add_string`[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Correct Offset Handling**: Reading length at offset [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m, then data at offset [0m[1;36m31[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m30[0m[39m+[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, properly skipping the length field[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Memory Safety**: Uses Wireshark's memory allocator with automatic lifecycle [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanagement[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Preserved Functionality[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The offset calculations in subsequent calls [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;36m40[0m[39m + buddyname_length` at line [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1979[0m[39m, `[0m[1;36m36[0m[39m + buddyname_length` at line [0m[1;36m1998[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain valid since `buddyname_length` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis still returned as an integer[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `col_append_fstr` calls at lines [0m[1;36m1982[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m2001[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m2002[0m[39m receive properly formatted [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnull-terminated strings[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `proto_tree_add_string` call at line [0m[1;36m2004[0m[39m receives a valid string pointer[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All existing protocol tree display functionality is preserved[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Alternative Mitigation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIf uint16_t is Required[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIf protocol analysis reveals that the length field is actually `uint16_t` in the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwire format, an alternative fix would be:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muint16_t buddyname_length = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_ntohs[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuddyname_length > [0m[1;36m255[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    buddyname_length = [0m[1;36m255[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Truncate to safe maximum[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Then proceed with safe extraction at offset+[0m[1;36m2[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHowever, based on the field definitions and reference implementations throughout [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe codebase, `uint8_t` is the correct type.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effect**: If any malformed packets have buddy names with length > [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m255[0m[39m, they will now cause exceptions instead of buffer overflows.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation**: This is the desired behavior - malformed packets should be rejected[0m [2m                [0m
